msg:Asia international hotel, 
This is the place to stay if you want a real feel for the warmth & charm of Rome & its people instead of a cold impersonal hotel. The owners & staff make you feel like part of their family and give wonderful support in every need of your visit ex. tours.& transportation. They speak very good English and their breakfast & coffee are excellent and will accommodate any request if possible. 

Excellent location, superb services, helpful staff, waht else do you need? Will definitely come again to this place. 

Very satisfied with the cleanliness of the hotel, the size of the room, the helpfulness of the staff at the front desk (all of them during our stay), they even go out of their way to guide you through the places to visit in Rome. The breakfast was to our expectation. The area is central even if one wishes to walk around. The only thing is that the room is hot, does not have enough light and no air comes in even if you open the window as it is sourrounded by buildings.

msg:I am in Room 2817. I want to report a weird acoustic sound. This is why I gave only three in "Facilities."

There is mid frequency (higher than what people would call rumble; low enough to feel the effect active noise cancellation of Bose QC20; more like pure sinusoidal tone type of sound, not white/pink noise type sound) constant acoustic noise. As I move my head, the noise disappears or appears - typical for a single tone wave in a room -. I could not find a specific equipment  (TV or lamp) that is generating this acoustic sound.

I did not request room change, as other rooms in the hotel building may have the same noise. It is not terribly loud, but it is definitely disturbing, not expected in a 5 star hotel.

The attached sound spectrum showing a peak in 700 - 800 Hz is from REW software with the built-in mic and sound card on my Huawei Matebook E.

We booked a business king room with a size of 36 square meters, but the current room is only about 20 square meters. There is a sink next to the bed, and a bathtub is placed in an open position across the sink. There is a toilet on the left side of the blue door and a bathroom on the right side. Because it is connected to the room, the light cannot be left on at night, otherwise it will be too bright when sleeping on the bed. Fortunately, I brought a night light.
Personally, I think this is one of the highlights of the hotel. This is the brightest room I have lived in so far. Most hotel rooms like to be extremely dim. Now most of the people who go out to play are families, both old and young. Are all the hotels receiving couples?
